Returns a formatted\n    45→    string suitable for terminal output per spec section 2.2 box layout.\n    46→\n    47→    Pure function: no I/O or side effects.\n    48→    \"\"\"\n    49→    blocking = [f for f in findings if f.severity == \"BLOCKING\"]\n    50→    warning = [f for f in findings if f.severity == \"WARNING\"]\n    51→    info = [f for f in findings if f.severity == \"INFO\"]\n    52→\n    53→    lines: list[str] = []\n    54→    lines.append(\"=\" * 60)\n    55→    lines.append(\"  VALIDATION SUMMARY\")\n    56→    lines.append(\"=\" * 60)\n    57→    lines.append(\"\")\n    58→\n    59→    total = len(findings)\n    60→    lines.append(f\"  Total findings: {total}\")\n    61→    lines.append(f\"  BLOCKING: {len(blocking)}  |  WARNING: {len(warning)}  |  INFO: {len(info)}\")\n    62→    lines.append(\"\")\n    63→\n    64→    if blocking:\n    65→        lines.append(\"  --- BLOCKING ---\")\n    66→        for f in blocking:\n    67→            lines.append(f\"  {f.id} | {f.description}\")\n    68→        lines.append(\"\")\n    69→\n    70→    if warning:\n    71→        lines.append(\"  --- WARNING ---\")\n    72→        for f in warning:\n    73→            lines.append(f\"  {f.id} | {f.description}\")\n    74→        lines.append(\"\")\n    75→\n    76→    if info:\n    77→        lines.append(\"  --- INFO ---\")\n    78→        for f in info:\n    79→            lines.append(f\"  {f.id} | {f.description}\")\n    80→        lines.append(\"\")\n    81→\n    82→    lines.append(\"=\" * 60)\n    83→    return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n    84→\n    85→\n    86→def should_skip_prompt(findings: list[Finding]) -> bool:\n    87→    \"\"\"Return True when prompt should be skipped (zero BLOCKING + zero WARNING).\n    88→\n    89→    Per spec section 2.2: when there are no BLOCKING and no WARNING findings,\n    90→    the prompt is auto-skipped.\n    91→\n    92→    Pure function: no I/O or side effects.\n    93→    \"\"\"\n    94→    blocking = sum(1 for f in findings if f.severity == \"BLOCKING\")\n    95→    warning = sum(1 for f in findings if f.severity == \"WARNING\")\n    96→    return blocking == 0 and warning == 0\n    97→\n    98→\n    99→def filter_findings(\n   100→    findings: list[Finding],\n   101→    scope: RemediationScope,\n   102→) -> tuple[list[Finding], list[Finding]]:\n   103→ 259→\n   260→def _build_steps(config: RoadmapConfig) -> list[Step | list[Step]]:\n   261→    \"\"\"Build the 9-step pipeline with parallel generate group.\n   262→\n   263→    Returns a list where 288→                encoding=\"utf-8\"\n   289→            )\n   290→        except OSError:\n   291→            retrospective_content = None\n   292→\n   293→    steps: list[Step | list[Step]] = [\n 318→            ),\n   319→            Step(\n   320→                id=f\"generate-{agent_b.id}\",\n   321→                prompt=build_generate_prompt(agent_b, extraction),\n   322→ inputs=[roadmap_a, roadmap_b],\n   338→            retry_limit=1,\n   339→        ),\n   340→        # Step 4: Debate\n   341→        Step(\n   342→            id=\"debate\",\n   343→ 394→\n   395→def _format_halt_output(results: list[StepResult], config: RoadmapConfig) -> str:\n   396→    \"\"\"Format HALT diagnostic output per spec section 6.2.\"\"\"\n   397→    failed = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n   398→    passed = [r for r in results if r.status == StepStatus.PASS]\n   399→    cancelled = [r for r in results if r.status == StepStatus.CANCELLED]\n   400→\n   401→    if not failed:\n   402→        return \"\"\n   403→\n   404→    fail = failed[-1]\n   405→    step = fail.step\n   406→\n   407→    # Calculate file details if output exists\n   408→    file_info = \"\"\n   409→    if step and step.output_file.exists():\n   410→        content = step.output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   411→        byte_count = len(content.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n   412→        line_count = len(content.splitlines())\n   413→        file_info = f\"  Output size: {byte_count} bytes ({line_count} lines)\\n\"\n   414→    elif step:\n   415→        file_info = \"  Output file: not created\\n\"\n   416→\n   417→    elapsed = f\"{fail.duration_seconds:.0f}s\"\n   418→\n   419→    lines = [\n   420→        f\"ERROR: Roadmap pipeline halted at step '{step.id}' (attempt {fail.attempt}/2)\",\n   421→        f\"  Gate failure: {fail.gate_failure_reason}\",\n   422→        f\"  Output file: {step.output_file}\",\n   423→        file_info.rstrip(),\n   424→        f\"  Step timeout: {step.timeout_seconds}s | Elapsed: {elapsed}\",\n   425→        \"\",\n   426→        f\"Completed steps: {', '.join(f'{r.step.id} (PASS, attempt {r.attempt})' for r in passed) or 'none'}\",\n   427→        f\"Failed step:     {step.id} ({fail.status.value}, attempt {fail.attempt})\",\n   428→    ]\n   429→\n   430→    # Collect skipped steps\n   431→    all_step_ids = _get_all_step_ids(config)\n   432→    executed_ids = {r.step.id for r in results}\n   433→    skipped_ids = [sid for sid in all_step_ids if sid not in executed_ids]\n   434→    if cancelled:\n   435→        skipped_ids = [r.step.id for r in cancelled] + skipped_ids\n   436→\n   437→    if skipped_ids:\n   438→        lines.append(f\"Skipped steps:   {', '.join(skipped_ids)}\")\n   439→\n   440→    lines.extend([\n   441→        \"\",\n   442→        \"To retry from this step:\",\n   443→        f\"  superclaude roadmap run {config.spec_file} --resume\",\n   444→        \"\",\n   445→        \"To inspect the failing output:\",\n   446→        f\"  cat {step.output_file}\",\n   447→    ])\n   448→\n   449→    return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n   450→\n   451→\n   452→def _get_all_step_ids(config: RoadmapConfig) -> list[str]:\n   453→    \"\"\"Get all step IDs in pipeline order.\"\"\"\n   454→    agent_a = config.agents[0]\n   455→    agent_b = config.agents[1] if len(config.agents) > 1 else config.agents[0]\n   456→    return [\n   457→        \"extract\",\n   458→        f\"generate-{agent_a.id}\",\n   459→ \"spec-fidelity\",\n   466→    ]\n   467→\n   468→\n   469→def _print_step_start(step: Step) -> None:\n   470→    \"\"\"Print progress output when a step starts.\"\"\"\n   471→    print(f\"[roadmap] Starting step: {step.id}\", flush=True)\n   472→\n   473→\n   474→def _print_step_complete(step: Step, result: StepResult) -> None:\n   475→    \"\"\"Print progress output when a step Reason: {result.gate_failure_reason}\", flush=True)\n   489→\n   490→\n   491→def _dry_run_output(steps: list[Step | list[Step]]) -> None:\n   492→    \"\"\"Print step plan and gate criteria for                _print_step_plan(step_num, s, parallel=True)\n   499→        else:\n   500→            step_num += 1\n   501→            _print_step_plan(step_num, entry)\n   502→\n   503→\n   504→def 521→\n   522→\n   523→def _save_state(config: RoadmapConfig, results: list[StepResult]) -> None:\n   524→    \"\"\"Write .roadmap-state.json to output_dir via atomic tmp + os.replace().\n   525→\n   526→    Preserves existing ``validation`` and ``fidelity_status`` keys if present.\n   527→    \"\"\"\n   528→    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n   529→    spec_hash = )\n   564→    if fidelity_result is not None:\n   565→        state[\"fidelity_status\"] = _derive_fidelity_status(fidelity_result)\n   566→    elif existing_fidelity is not None:\n   567→ \"\"\"Derive fidelity_status enum from a spec-fidelity StepResult.\n   574→\n   575→    Returns one of: 'pass', 'fail', 'skipped', 'degraded'.\n   576→    \"\"\"\n   577→    if result.status == StepStatus.PASS:\n   578→        # Check if the output indicates degraded mode\n   579→        if result.step and result.step.output_file.exists():\n   580→            content = 584→    if result.status == StepStatus.SKIPPED:\n   585→        return \"skipped\"\n   586→    if result.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT):\n   587→        return \"fail\"\n   588→    return \"skipped\"\n   589→\n   590→\n   591→def generate_degraded_report(\n   592→    output_file: Path,\n   593→    failed_agent: str,\n   594→    failure_reason: str,\n   595→) -> None:\n   596→    \"\"\"Generate a degraded fidelity report when the agent fails.\n   597→\n   598→    Produces a report with validation_complete=false and\n   599→    fidelity_check_attempted=true so the \"---\\n\"\n   614→        \"\\n\"\n   615→        \"## Degraded Fidelity Report\\n\"\n   616→        \"\\n\"\n   617→        \"Spec-fidelity validation could not be completed.\\n\"\n   618→ 634→\n   635→\n   636→def write_state(state: dict, path: Path) -> None:\n   637→    \"\"\"Write state dict to path atomically via tmp file + os.replace().\"\"\"\n   638→    import os as _os\n   639→\n   640→    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n   641→    tmp = path.with_suffix(\".tmp\")\n   642→    tmp.write_text(json.dumps(state, indent=2), encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   643→    _os.replace(str(tmp), str(path))\n   644→\n   645→\n   646→def read_state(path: Path) -> dict | None:\n   647→    \"\"\"Read state from path with graceful recovery on missing/malformed files.\"\"\"\n   648→    if not path.exists():\n   649→        return None\n   650→    try:\n   651→        text = path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   652→        if not text.strip():\n   653→            return None\n   654→        return json.loads(text)\n   655→    except (json.JSONDecodeError, OSError):\n   656→        return None\n   657→\n   658→\n   659→def apply_decomposition_pass(deliverables: list[Deliverable]) -> list[Deliverable]:\n   660→    \"\"\"Post-generation decomposition pass for the roadmap pipeline.\n   661→\n   662→    Runs after deliverable generation, before output formatting.\n   663→    Splits behavioral deliverables into Implement/Verify pairs.\n   664→\n   665→    Idempotent: running twice produces identical results because\n   666→    already-decomposed deliverables (IDs ending .a/.b) are skipped.\n   667→\n   668→    Preserves milestone-internal ordering: deliverables within each\n   669→    milestone maintain their relative order after decomposition.\n   670→    \"\"\"\n   671→    return decompose_deliverables(deliverables)\n   672→\n   673→\n   674→def execute_roadmap(config: RoadmapConfig, resume: bool = False, no_validate: bool = False) -> None:\n   675→    \"\"\"Execute the roadmap generation pipeline.\n   676→\n   677→    Builds the step list, handles --dry-run and --resume, then\n   678→    delegates to execute_pipeline() with roadmap_run_step.\n   679→\n   680→    After all 9 steps pass, auto-invokes validation unless\n   681→    --no-validate is set or --resume halted on a failed step.\n   682→\n   683→    Note: --no-validate does NOT skip the spec-fidelity step\n   684→    (FR-010, AC-005). It only skips the post-pipeline validation\n   685→    subsystem.\n   686→    \"\"\"\n   687→    config.output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n   688→\n   689→    steps =  701→\n   702→    # Execute pipeline\n   703→    results = execute_pipeline(\n   704→        steps=steps,\n   705→        config=config,\n   706→        run_step=roadmap_run_step,\n   707→ config)\n   718→        print(halt_msg, file=sys.stderr)\n   719→        sys.exit(1)\n   720→\n   721→    print(f\"\\n[roadmap] Pipeline complete: {len(results)} steps passed\", flush=True)\n   722→\n _save_validation_status(config, \"skipped\")\n   727→        return\n   728→\n   729→    # Check if validation already completed (--resume path)\n   730→    if resume:\n   731→        state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n   732→        state = read_state(state_file)\n   733→        if state and \"validation\" in state:\n   734→            saved = state[\"validation\"]\n   735→            if saved.get(\"status\") in (\"pass\", \"fail\"):\n   736→                print(\n   737→                    f\"[roadmap] Validation already completed ({saved['status']}), _save_validation_status(\n   746→    config: RoadmapConfig,\n   747→    status: str,\n   748→) -> None:\n   749→    \"\"\"Update .roadmap-state.json with validation status.\n   750→\n   751→    Adds \"\"\"Auto-invoke validation after a successful roadmap pipeline run.\n   773→\n   774→    Inherits --model, --max-turns, --debug from the parent roadmap config.\n   775→    Default agent count for Your task is to apply specific, \"\n        \"targeted fixes to a single file based on validation findings.\"\n    )\n    lines.append(\"\")\n\n    # Target File section\n    lines.append(\"## Target File\")\n    lines.append(\"\")\n    lines.append(f\"`{target_file}`\")\n    lines.append(\"\")\n\n    # Findings to Fix section\n    lines.append(\"## Findings to Fix\")\n    lines.append(\"\")\n    for f in findings:\n        lines.append(f\"### {f.id} [{f.severity}]\")\n        lines.append(\"\")\n        lines.append(f\"- **ID**: {f.id}\")\n        lines.append(f\"- **Severity**: {f.severity}\")\n        lines.append(f\"- **Description**: {f.description}\")\n        lines.append(f\"- **Location**: {f.location}\")\n        lines.append(f\"- **Evidence**: {f.evidence}\")\n        lines.append(f\"- **Fix Guidance**: {f.fix_guidance}\")\n        lines.append(\"\")\n\n    # Constraints section\n    lines.append(\"## Constraints\")\n    lines.append(\"\")\n    lines.append(f\"1. _log.warning(\n                \"Finding %s references non-allowlisted files: %s -- SKIPPING\",\n                finding.id,\n                \", \".join(non_allowed),\n            )\n            rejected.append(finding)\n        else:\n            allowed.append(finding)\n\n    return allowed, rejected\n\n\ndef _basename(path: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Extract basename from a path, handling both absolute and relative paths.\"\"\"\n    return Path(path).name\n\n\n# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n# T04.05 -- Parallel Agent Execution with ClaudeProcess\n# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n\n\ndef _run_agent_for_file(\n    target_file: str,\n    findings: list[Finding],\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    output_dir: Path,\n) -> tuple[str, int]:\n    \"\"\"Spawn a ClaudeProcess for a single file group.\n\n    Returns (target_file, exit_code) tuple.\n    \"\"\"\n    prompt = build_remediation_prompt(target_file, findings)\n    output_file = output_dir / f\"remediate-{Path(target_file).stem}.md\"\n    error_file = output_file.with_suffix(\".err\")\n\n    proc = ClaudeProcess(\n        prompt=prompt,\n        output_file=output_file,\n        error_file=error_file,\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=config.model,\n        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n        timeout_seconds=_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,\n        output_format=\"text\",\n        extra_args=[\"--file\", target_file],\n    )\n\n    proc.start()\n    exit_code = proc.wait()\n    return target_file, exit_code\n\n\ndef _run_agent_with_retry(\n    target_file: str,\n    findings: list[Finding],\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    output_dir: Path,\n    all_target_files: list[str],\n) -> tuple[str, int, int]:\n    \"\"\"Run agent with single retry on failure per NFR-002.\n\n    On first failure, restores snapshot and retries once.\n    Returns (target_file, exit_code, attempt_count).\n    \"\"\"\n    # Attempt 1\n    target, exit_code = _run_agent_for_file(\n        target_file, findings, config, output_dir\n    )\n\n    if exit_code == 0:\n        return target, exit_code, 1\n\n    _log.warning(\n        \"Agent for %s failed (exit %d), restoring snapshot and retrying\",\n        target_file,\n        exit_code,\n    )\n\n    # Restore snapshot before retry\n    snapshot = Path(f\"{target_file}.pre-remediate\")\n    if snapshot.exists():\n        os.replace(str(snapshot), str(target_file))\n        # Re-create snapshot for the retry\n        content = Path(target_file).read_bytes()\n        tmp = Path(f\"{target_file}.pre-remediate.tmp\")\n        tmp.write_bytes(content)\n        os.replace(str(tmp), str(snapshot))\n\n    # Attempt 2\n    target, findings_by_file: dict[str, list[Finding]],\n    executor: ThreadPoolExecutor | None = None,\n) -> list[Finding]:\n    \"\"\"Handle agent failure: rollback ALL files, mark findings FAILED.\n\n    Spec section 2.3.8 five-step procedure:\n    1. Halt remaining agents (via executor shutdown)\n    2. Rollback ALL target files from .pre-remediate snapshots\n    3. Mark all findings for failed agent as FAILED\n    4. Mark cross-file findings involving failed file as FAILED\n    5. Set remediate step to FAIL\n\n    Returns list of all findings with updated statuses.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Step 1: Halt remaining agents\n    if executor is not None:\n        executor.shutdown(wait=False, cancel_futures=True)\n\n    # Step 2: Rollback ALL target files\n    restore_from_snapshots(all_target_files)\n    _log.info(\"Rolled back all %d target files\", len(all_target_files))\n\n    # Steps 3-4: Mark findings as FAILED\n    all_findings: list[Finding] = []\n    for file_path, file_findings in findings_by_file.items():\n        for finding in file_findings:\n            if finding.id not in {f.id for f in all_findings}:\n                # Delete snapshots\n    cleanup_snapshots(all_target_files)\n\n    # Mark all agent-targeted findings as FIXED (preserve SKIPPED)\n    all_findings: list[Finding] = []\n    seen_ids: set[str] = set()\n    for file_findings in findings_by_file.values():\n        for finding in file_findings:\n            if finding.id not in seen_ids:\n                seen_ids.add(finding.id)\n                if finding.status == \"PENDING\":\n                    finding.status = \"FIXED\"\n                # Build status lookup\n    status_map: dict[str, str] = {f.id: f.status for f in findings}\n\n    # Update frontmatter counts\n    content = _update_frontmatter_counts(content, findings)\n\n    # Update finding entries\n    content = _update_finding_entries(content, status_map)\n\n    # Atomic write\n    tmp = path.with_suffix(path.suffix + \".tmp\")\n    tmp.write_text(content, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    os.replace(str(tmp), str(path))\n\n    _log.info(\"Updated remediation tasklist: %s\", tasklist_path)\n\n\ndef _update_frontmatter_counts(content: str, findings: list[Finding]) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Update YAML frontmatter counts based on final statuses.\"\"\"\n    actionable = sum(1 for f in findings if f.status in (\"FIXED\", \"FAILED\", \"PENDING\"))\n    skipped = sum(1 for f in findings if f.status == \"SKIPPED\")\n\n    content = re.sub(\n        r\"^actionable: \\d+\",\n        f\"actionable: {actionable}\",\n        content,\n        flags=re.MULTILINE,\n    )\n    content = re.sub(\n        r\"^skipped: \\d+\",\n        f\"skipped: {skipped}\",\n        content,\n        flags=re.MULTILINE,\n    )\n    return content\n\n\ndef _update_finding_entries(content: str, status_map: dict[str, str]) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Update checklist entries with final statuses.\"\"\"\n    for finding_id, status in status_map.items():\n        if status == \"FIXED\":\n            #
